<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 7; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(7);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView', GridHeight: '300', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '300', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

                gridName: 'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView', GridHeight: '300', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',
                selectedRecords: $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView() {
        var gridName = 'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView');

        if (parseBool("True")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

    $(document).ready(function () {

        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "PRApprovalsDataView");

        $("#btnCancelRequisition__PRApprovalsDataView").click(function () {
            var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView");
            if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
                return;
            }
            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Cancel", "Are you sure you would like to cancel this Requisition request?", function () { cancelLR(selectedRowIds); });
        });
        var openPopup = $("#FromPopup").val();
        var prId = $("#prID").val();

        if(openPopup == "True")
        {
            var AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView.dataSource.bind("change", function () {
                if (AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView.dataSource.data().length &gt; 0) {
                    AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView.dataSource.unbind("change");
                    var grid = $("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView");
                    var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    EditPurchaseRequisitionFinsWindow(prId, aptaDataViewSelection);
                }
            });

        }

    });

    $("#btnView__PRApprovalsDataView").click(function () {
        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowId)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        NavigateTo("/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/MyDetails" + "?id=" + selectedRowId + "&amp;statusType=" + '3' + "&amp;returnScreen=&amp;enableAccountCode=&amp;isViewOnly=true");

    });

    });


    $("#btnAdd__PRApprovalsDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var id, data, options;
        var approverId = "";

        id = approverId + "|" + '3';

        data = { Id: id, origin: 1 };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/CreateMyRequisitionPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowRequisition")
        .SetIsModal(true)
        .SetContent(options)
        .SetWidth(1000)
        .SetHeight("90%")
        .SetonClose(ReturnFromRequisitionScreen)
        .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
        .SetTitle('Add Purchase Requisition');
    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PurchaseRequisitionView", null);

    });

    function EditPurchaseRequisitionPopup(Id) {
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        EditPurchaseRequisitionFinsWindow(Id, aptaDataViewSelection);
    }

    function EditPurchaseRequisitionFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {

        var approverId = "";

        var data, options;

        data = { Id: id, origin: 1, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3' };

        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowRequisition")
       .SetIsModal(true)
       .SetContent(options)
       .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
       .SetTitle('Edit Purchase Requisition')
       .SetonClose(ReturnFromRequisitionScreen)
       .SetWidth(1000)
       .SetHeight("90%")
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PurchaseRequisitionView", null);
    }

    $("#btnEdit__PRApprovalsDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            EditPurchaseRequisitionFinsWindow("", aptaDataViewSelection);
        }
    });


    function ReturnFromRequisitionScreen() {
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "PRApprovalsDataView");
    }


    $('#btnEditAll__PRApprovalsDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        if (grid.dataSource.data().length &lt;= 0) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "There are currently no items in the list to Edit.", null);
            return;
        }
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (selectedRowId !== "-1") {
            $('.selectAll__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').click();
        }
        $('#btnEdit__PRApprovalsDataView').click();
    });

      
    function ReturnFromRequisition() {
        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if(grid != null)
            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
    }


    $("#btnDelete__PRApprovalsDataView").click(function (e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        if (ValidateGridSelection("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView", true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected requisitions?", DeleteRequisitions);
        }

    });

    $("#btnEdit__PRApprovalsDataView_Popup").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0) {
            var passValue = selectedRowIds.split(',');
            window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/MyDetails?Id=" + passValue[0] + "&amp;statusType=" + '3' + "&amp;ReturnScreen=Manage";
        }
    });


    function GotoPurchaseOrder(poNumber) {
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/PurchaseRequisitionItemsGoToSource',
            cache: false,
            data: { purchaseorderNumber: poNumber },
            type: 'GET',

            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {

                    if (result.Success === true) {
                        if (result.IsTargetPopup) {
                            ShowPODetailPopup(result.Url, result.TargetPopupTitle);

                        }
                        else {
                            window.location.href = result.Url;
                        }
                    }
                    else {

                        gotoSourceInProgress = false;
                        ShowOkDialog('Purchase Order', 'Purchase order not found');
                    }
                }
            }

        });
    }

    $("#btnCopyRequisition__PRApprovalsDataView").click(function () {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (ValidateGridSelection("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView", false, "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.")) {

            var data = "selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds;
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                async: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/CopyRequisition",
                data: data,
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result == "") {
                        ReturnFromAction();
                        ShowAjaxMessage("Purchase Requisition copied successfully.", "success");
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error");
                    }
                    //ResizeGridOnMessage(true);
                },
                error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                    console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                }
            });
        }
    });

    function ReturnFromAction() {
        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");

    }
    function ResizeGridOnMessage(doresize) {
        if (doresize) {
            ResizeGridForAutoHeight("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView");
        }
    }

    function cancelLR(requestId) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var arrPassValue = requestId.split('~');
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/CancelRequisition",
            data: { requestId: arrPassValue[0], approvalType: '3' },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                    var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    grid.dataSource.read();
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function RefreshOnDeleteRequisitions(selectedRowId) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();

        $("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/MultipleDelete',
                 { massOpertaionId: massOperationId, selectedRowIds: selectedRowId },
                'AdminRequisition', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function DeleteRequisitions() {
        var dataView = 'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView';

        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnDeleteRequisitions(selectedRowId); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    }

    function OnCheckChange_ApproverList() {
        //OnSelectedIndexChange_ApproverList();
    }

    

    var submitForAllNo = false;
    var submitForAllYes = false;
    $("#btnSubmitRequisition__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        submitForAllNo = false;
        submitForAllYes = false;

        if (!$("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        ShowYesNoDialog('Confirm Submit', 'Are you sure you want to submit the selected requisition(s)?', function () {
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition("-1", false, false, 'AdminRequisition'); });
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
        });

    });

    function RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(requisitionId, overbudget, moveNext, key) {
        var operationResultId = GetMassActionId();

        $("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/SubmitMassRequsition',
                     { requisitionId: requisitionId, overBudget: overbudget, moveNext: moveNext, operationResultId: operationResultId, key: key },
                key, function (result) {
                    if (result.Success == 1) {
                        RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, false, key);

                    } else if (result.Success == 3) {

                        if (submitForAllYes === true) {
                            RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, true, false, key);
                        }
                        else if (submitForAllNo === true) {
                            RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, true, key);
                        }
                        else {

                            if ('True' == 'True') {
                                result.Message += "&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Do you wish to continue?"
                                ShowYesNoDialogWithCheckBox("Admin Purchase Requisitions", result.Message, function (e) { RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, true, false, key); submitForAllYes = e; }, function (e) { RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, true, key); submitForAllNo = e; });
                            }
                            else {
                                // create an appropriate error message
                                result.Message += "&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Purchase Request cannot be submitted."
                                ShowOkDialog("Admin Purchase Requisitions", result.Message, null);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    else if (result.Success == 4) {

                        //4 indicates process end,
                        submitForAllNo = false;
                        submitForAllYes = false;
                        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                        ShowResultGrid();
                    }
                    else {
                        RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, false, key);

                    }
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults", false);

    }

    function ShowResultGrid() {
        ShowMassActionResultsPopup('popupwindowMassActionResults');
    }

    $("#btnAttachments__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").click(function () {

        if (ValidateGridSelection("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView", false, "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.")) {
            var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView");
            NavigateTo("/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/PRAttachments" + "/" + selectedRowIds);
        }

    });

    $("#btnPrint__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").click(function () {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowPrintPRs")
                .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/PrintPurchaseRequisitionPrintSetup?" + "PRIdList=" + selectedRowIds + "&amp;dataView=AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView" + "&amp;PrintRequisitionPopup=AdminRequisition__PrintPurchaseRequisitionPrintSetup" })
                .SetIsModal(true).SetWidth(650).SetHeight(150)
                .SetTitle("Print Purchase Requisition");
    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }

<script>
    var PRloadTabRequestedItems = true;
    var PRloadTabApprovalHistory = true;
    var PRloadTabAttachmentView = true;

	function onActivate(e) {
        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        var activeTabStripText = $("#tabstripPR").data("FINSUITabStrip").GetActiveTabText()
        if (activeTabStripText == 'Requested Items') {
			if (PRloadTabRequestedItems) {
				if (PRloadTabRequestedItems &amp;&amp; '4178' &gt; 0) {
                    LoadGridOnDemand__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView();
					PRloadTabRequestedItems = false;
                }
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup", "PurchaseRequisitionView", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView");
        }

        else if (activeTabStripText == 'Approval History') {
            if (PRloadTabApprovalHistory) {
                var grid = $("#ApprovalTransactionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                grid.dataSource.read();
                PRloadTabApprovalHistory = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup", "PurchaseRequisitionView", null);
        }

        else if (activeTabStripText == 'Attached Files') {
            if (PRloadTabAttachmentView) {
				LoadGridOnDemand__AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3();
				var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3").data("kendoGrid");
                grid.dataSource.read();
                PRloadTabAttachmentView = false;
            }
			ResizeGridForAutoHeight("#AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3")
			RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3__PurchaseRequisition", "AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3__PurchaseRequisition");
        }

    }

    $("#btnCancel__PurchaseRequisitionView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        closRequisitioneWindow(e);

    });

    function closRequisitioneWindow(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        var grid = $("#"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoGrid");
        if(grid != null)
            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
    }

    function OnRequisitionerChange() {
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/RefreshShipToList',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: { requisitionerID: $("#RequisitionerId").data("kendoComboBox").value() },
            success: function (result) {
                if (result !== null &amp;&amp; result.responseText != "0") {
                    $("#DestinationId").data("kendoComboBox").value(result.responseText);
                }
                else {
                    $("#DestinationId").data("kendoComboBox").value('');
                }
            },
            error: function (result) {
            }
        });
    }

    function OnChange_PRType() {
        OnPRTypeChage(false);
    }

    function OnPRTypeChage(init) {
        $("#WarehouseId").data("FINSComboBox").SetVisible(false);
        $("#SuggestedOrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").SetVisible(true);
        var approvaltype = $("#PRType").data("kendoComboBox").value();
        if (approvaltype != null) {
            if (approvaltype === 'L') {
                approvaltype = 4;
                var combobox = $("#WarehouseId").data("kendoComboBox");
                if (combobox.dataSource._data.length == 1) {
                    combobox.select(0);
                }
                $("#WarehouseId").data("FINSComboBox").SetVisible(true);
            }
            else if (approvaltype === 'W') {
                approvaltype = 5;
                var combobox = $("#WarehouseId").data("kendoComboBox");
                if (combobox.dataSource._data.length == 1) {
                    combobox.select(0);
                }
                $("#WarehouseId").data("FINSComboBox").SetVisible(true);
                $("#SuggestedOrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").SetVisible(false);
            }
            else {
                approvaltype = 3;
            }
        }

        if ('Admin Purchase Requisitions' === 'Admin Purchase Requisitions') {
            $.ajax({
                url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/RefreshApproverListPopup',
                cache: false,
                dataType: 'JSON',
                data: { approvalType: approvaltype },
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result !== null) {

                        var dropDown = $("#ApproverId").data("kendoComboBox");
                        if (dropDown != null) {
                            dropDown.dataSource.data(result);
                            dropDown.refresh();
                            var len = dropDown.dataSource.data().length;
                            if (len &gt;= 1) {
                                dropDown.value('');
                            }
                            else {
                                dropDown.value('');
                            }
                        }

                        OnSelectedIndexChangePopup_ApproverListComboBox();
                    }
                },
                error: function (result) {
                }
            });
        }
        else if (init == false) {
            ReloadRequisitioner('');
        }
    }

    function OnSelectedIndexChangePopup_ApproverListComboBox() {
        var approverId = null;

        var dropDown = $("#ApproverId").data("kendoComboBox");
        if (dropDown != null) {
            let tempApproverId = dropDown.value();
            if (tempApproverId != null) {
                let tempArray = tempApproverId.split("~");
                if (tempArray.length &gt; 0) {
                    approverId = tempArray[0];
                }
            }
        }
        ReloadRequisitioner(approverId);
    }

    function ReloadRequisitioner(approver) {
        let cbRqn = $("#RequisitionerId").data("FINSComboBox");
        if (cbRqn != null) {
            let showAllRequisitioners = false;
            let chk = $("#ShowAllRequisitioners");
            if (chk != null) {
                showAllRequisitioners = chk.prop('checked') ? true : false;
            }
            cbRqn.DataParameters.ShowAllRequisitioners = showAllRequisitioners;
            cbRqn.DataParameters.ApproverId = approver;

            var approvaltype = $("#PRType").data("kendoComboBox").value();
            if (approvaltype === 'L') {
                cbRqn.DataParameters.RequisitionerType = 'ReplenishmentRequisition';
            }
            else if (approvaltype === 'W') {
                cbRqn.DataParameters.RequisitionerType = 'WarehouseRequisition';
            }
            else {
                cbRqn.DataParameters.RequisitionerType = 'PurchaseRequisition';
            }

            cbRqn.ReloadData();
            if (cbRqn.Value != null &amp;&amp; !cbRqn.DoesValueExistInSource(cbRqn.Value)) {
                cbRqn.SetValue("");
            }
            if (showAllRequisitioners || approver) { cbRqn.SetValue(""); }
        }
    }

    function OnCheckChange_ApproverList() {
        OnSelectedIndexChangePopup_ApproverListComboBox();
    }

    function OnCheckChange_AllRequisitions() {
        var isChecked = $('#ShowAllRequisitioners').prop('checked') ? true : false;

        if (isChecked) {
            $("#ApproverId").data("kendoComboBox").enable(false);
            ReloadRequisitioner('');
        }
        else {
            $("#ApproverId").data("kendoComboBox").enable();
            OnSelectedIndexChangePopup_ApproverListComboBox();
        }
    }

    function ProcessCartItems(cartID) {
        var prID = '4178';
        NavigateTo('ProcessPunchoutMessage' + "?cartId=" + cartID + "&amp;prID=" + prID + "&amp;statusType=" + '3');
    }

    function DontProcessCartItems(cartID) {
        var prID = '4178';
        var data = { prID: prID, cartId: cartID };

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/DontProcessCart',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    if (result !== "") {

                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function GotoPurchaseOrder(poNumber) {
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/PurchaseRequisitionGoToSource',
            cache: false,
            data: { purchaseorderNumber: poNumber },
            type: 'GET',

            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {

                    if (result.Success === true) {
                        if (result.IsTargetPopup) {
                            OpenPODetailPopupfromPR(result.Url, result.TargetPopupTitle);

                        }
                        else {
                            window.location.href = result.Url;
                        }
                    }
                    else {

                        gotoSourceInProgress = false;
                        ShowOkDialog('Purchase Order', 'Purchase order not found');
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function ResizeGridOnMessage(doReSize) {
        if ('Admin Purchase Requisitions' === 'Admin Purchase Requisitions') {
            NavigateTo('' + "?Id=" + '4178' + "&amp;statusType=" + '3');
        }
        else {
            NavigateTo('' + "?Id=" + '4178' + "&amp;statusType=" + '3' + "&amp;returnScreen=" + 'MyPR');
        }
    }

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView', GridHeight: '300', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '300', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

            cache: false,
            data: {
                gridName: 'PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView', GridHeight: '300', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'False',
                selectedRecords: $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divPurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView() {
        var gridName = 'PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView');

        if (parseBool("False")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divPurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowAttachmentFramework__PurchaseRequisition")
                      .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/AddAttachment?ScreenName=PurchaseRequisition" + "&amp;ObjectKey1=4178" + "&amp;ObjectKey2=-1" + "&amp;ObjectKey3=" })
                      .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(ReturnFromAttachmentPopup__PurchaseRequisition)
                      .SetTitle("Add Attachment")
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "frmAttachment__PurchaseRequisition", "AttachmentFrameworkDataView__PurchaseRequisition");
        });

        $("#btnEdit__AttachmentFrameworkDataView__PurchaseRequisition").click(function () {
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
                return;
            }

            var gridData = grid.dataSource.data();
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; gridData.length; i++) {
                if (gridData[i].Id == selectedRowIds &amp;&amp; gridData[i].syViewFileAttachments__ScreenName != 'PurchaseRequisition') {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Linked attachment cannot be edited", "error");
                    return;
                }
            }

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowAttachmentFramework__PurchaseRequisition")
                      .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditAttachment?FileId=" + selectedRowIds })
                      .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(ReturnFromAttachmentPopup__PurchaseRequisition)
                      .SetTitle("Edit Attachment")
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "frmAttachment__PurchaseRequisition", "AttachmentFrameworkDataView__PurchaseRequisition");
        });

        $("#btnDelete__AttachmentFrameworkDataView__PurchaseRequisition").click(function () {
            var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0) {
                ShowYesNoDialog('Confirm Delete', 'Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?', DeleteAttachments);
            }
            else {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            }
        });

        function DeleteAttachments() {
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(MassActionResultRefresh).
    SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen);
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
        }

        function MassActionResultRefresh()
        {
            var massActionId = GetMassActionId();
            $("#divAttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/GridConfig/DeleteAttachment',
				{ massOpertaionId: massActionId, dataView: "AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3" },
                    '', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3").data("kendoGrid");
                        //removing selection from the attributes.
                        grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected", "");
                        grid.thead.find("tr .selectAll__AttachmentFrameworkDataView").attr("checked", false);
                        SetGridSelectedRecords("AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3", "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                        //refresh grid
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
        }

        $("#btnView__AttachmentFrameworkDataView__PurchaseRequisition").click(function () {

            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
                return;
			}
			window.location.href = "/QAAutom/GridConfig/ViewAttachment" + "?dataView=AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3";

        });

    });
</script>

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__ApprovalTransactionsDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__ApprovalTransactionsDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'ApprovalTransactionsDataView', GridHeight: '300', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__ApprovalTransactionsDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__ApprovalTransactionsDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '300', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__ApprovalTransactionsDataView').click(function () {

        $("#settingsWindow__ApprovalTransactionsDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__ApprovalTransactionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'ApprovalTransactionsDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__ApprovalTransactionsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__ApprovalTransactionsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__ApprovalTransactionsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___ApprovalTransactionsDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'False' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("ApprovalTransactionsDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__ApprovalTransactionsDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__ApprovalTransactionsDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__ApprovalTransactionsDataView() {
        var gridName = 'ApprovalTransactionsDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_ApprovalTransactionsDataView');

        if (parseBool("False")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "ApprovalTransactionsDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_ApprovalTransactionsDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__ApprovalTransactionsDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    });

<script>
    function getLocalDateTime(serverDate) {
        if (serverDate != null &amp;&amp; serverDate != "") {
            var serverDateTime = new Date(serverDate);
            var d = new Date();
            var n = d.getTimezoneOffset();
            var hours = n / 60;
            var minutes = n % 60;
            hours = hours * -1;
            minutes = minutes * -1;
            serverDateTime.setHours(serverDateTime.getHours() + hours);
            serverDateTime.setMinutes(serverDateTime.getMinutes() + minutes);
            var dateClientSide = serverDateTime;
            return kendo.toString(dateClientSide, ('MM/dd/yyyy  hh:mm  tt'));
        }
        return "";
    }
</script>

<script>

    $('#btnSaveAndSubmit__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        ShowYesNoDialog('Confirm Submit', 'Are you sure you would like to submit the selected requisition?', function () {
            SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, "Submit")
        });

    });

    function SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, operation) {
        $("#PROperation").val(0);
        $("#PRIsSubmit").val(true);
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
        var destinationID = $("#DestinationId").val();

        var rName;
        var requisitionerId;
        var validationMessage = '';

        if ('4178' &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; ('Admin Purchase Requisitions' == 'Admin Purchase Requisitions' || 'Admin Purchase Requisitions' == 'My Purchase Requisition Approvals')) {
            rName = $('#RequestorName').val();
            requisitionerId = '247af42e-6fa6-44ee-9ac9-850b4c6e8a3c';
            $("#RequestorName").data("FINSUITextInput").SetValue(rName);
            $('#RequisitionerId').val(requisitionerId);
        }
        else {
            rName = $('#RequisitionerId').data("kendoComboBox").text();
            requisitionerId = $('#RequisitionerId').data("kendoComboBox").value();
            $("#RequisitionerId").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue(requisitionerId);
            $('#RequestorName').val(rName);
        }

        if (typeof destinationID == 'undefined' || destinationID == '')
            validationMessage += 'Ship To is required' + '&lt;br /&gt;';
        if (typeof requisitionerId == 'undefined' || requisitionerId == '')
            validationMessage += 'Requisitioner Name is required.' + '&lt;br /&gt;';

        if (validationMessage != '') {

            ShowAjaxMessage(validationMessage, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            return;
        }

        var form = $("#RequisitionDetails");
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: form.attr('action'),
            data: form.serialize(),
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success == true) {

                    if (operation == "Submit")
                    {
                        SubmitRequisitions(false, e);
                    }

                    else if (operation == "Approve")
                    {
                        ApproveRequisitionOnPopup(e);
                    }

                    else if (operation == "Disapprove")
                    {
                        RefreshPopupAfterDisapproveRequisition(e);
                    }

                    else if (operation == "CopyRequisition")
                    {
                        CopyRequisitionPopup(e);
                    }

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }

            }
        });
    }

    function SubmitRequisitions(overBudget, e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
        var data = { overBudget: overBudget, requisitionId: '4178' };
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/SubmitRequisition",
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {

                if (result.success == true) {
                    var navigationID = 0;

                    if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').is(":visible")){
                        navigationID = '4178';
                    }
                    else{
                        navigationID = '';
                    }
                    var aptaDataViewSelection;
                    var grid = $("#"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                    if(grid != null)
                    {
                        aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    }
                    else{
                        aptaDataViewSelection = null;
                    }

                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : navigationID, origin:'PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
                else if (result.success == false) {
                    if ('True' == 'True') {
                        result.Message += "&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Do you wish to continue?"
                        ShowYesNoDialog("Purchase Requisition", result.Message, function () { SubmitRequisitions(true, e); });
                    }
                    else {
                        result.Message += "&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Purchase Requisition cannot be submitted."
                        ShowOkDialog("Purchase Requisition", result.Message, null);
                    }
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            },
            error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
            }
        });
    }
